traditional face-to-face classes.

course

and

Online BBA courses in the College of Business and Economics are charged separate tuition from the
traditional face-to-face classes.
The
online BBA
course
tuition
is
not
included in
the 12-credit fixed tuition cost for traditional classes.
The additional
tuition charge is $389 per credit.
Students must have
access to the internet
and
an internet browser. A webcam may be required for remote exam monitoring.

traditional face-to-face classes.
The
online BBA
course
tuition
is
not
included in
the 12-credit fixed tuition cost for traditional classes.

tuition charge is $389 per credit.
Students must have
access to the internet
and
an internet browser. A webcam may be required for remote exam monitoring.

BIOLOGY 250/GEOLGY 250
Requirement Designation
GE Lab Science
Combined Section ID
0004(BIOLOGY/ GEOLGY
250-01) -
GEOLGY 250(#1496)
The
course consists of
two
parts
1) online coursework and 2) three weeks of faculty-led group
travel
on
August 2-22, 2021. Students with disabilities may
be
accommodated. Biology majors/minors, Environmental Studies majors/minors and Geology/Geography
majors/minors should take BIO/GLG 451. Contact Kari Borne
(bornek@uww.edu or 262-472-1003)
for an application or Professor Clokey (clokeyg@uww.edu or 262- 472-5140) for academic requirements. Permission to add or
withdraw from the course must be obtained from the instructor and will be posted in WINS by the travel study office. Go to http
//www.uww.edu/ce/travel for
more
information on due dates,
itinerary, and course fees.
This
is
a hybrid course which
will have both classroom meetings and online instruction. Further
information will be given before the first day of class.

is
a hybrid course which

atomic bomb was one of the most important objects
of

in

behind how it worked, and the moral issues raised by such
a
device.
Great
stories and IS credit too!
